      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Civilian_operators">
        Civilian operators
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mikoyan-Gurevich_MiG-21&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Civilian operators">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       According to the
       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Aviation_Administration" title="Federal Aviation Administration">
        United States Federal Aviation Administration (FAA)
       </a>
       , there were 44 privately owned MiG-21s in the U.S. in 2012
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">
        <a href="#cite_note-137">
         [134]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       By 2013
       <a href="/wiki/Draken_International" title="Draken International">
        Draken International
       </a>
       acquired 30 MiG-21bis/UM, mostly ex-Polish.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">
        <a href="#cite_note-138">
         [135]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In 2017 it operates 30 MiGs.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">
        <a href="#cite_note-139">
         [136]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Use_as_space_launch_platform">
        Use as space launch platform
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mikoyan-Gurevich_MiG-21&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Use as space launch platform">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Premier Space Systems in Hillsboro, Oregon, USA is currently conducting flight tests for NanoLaunch, a project to launch suborbital
       <a href="/wiki/Sounding_rocket" title="Sounding rocket">
        sounding rockets
       </a>
       from MiG-21s flying over the Pacific Ocean.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Vintage_140-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Vintage-140">
         [137]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span id="Specifications_.28MiG-21-93.29">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Specifications_(MiG-21-93)">
        Specifications (MiG-21-93)
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mikoyan-Gurevich_MiG-21&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Specifications (MiG-21-93)">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MiG-21.svg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="900" data-file-width="1554" height="127" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/MiG-21.svg/220px-MiG-21.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/MiG-21.svg/330px-MiG-21.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/MiG-21.svg/440px-MiG-21.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MiG-21.svg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Mikoyan-Gurevich MiG-21PF
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p style="font-size: 90%; margin:0; padding: .2em">
       <i>
        Data from
       </i>
       Gordon,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gordon_2008_1-35">
        <a href="#cite_note-Gordon_2008-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       deagel.com
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">
        <a href="#cite_note-141">
         [138]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       <span style="font-size: 120%;">
        <b>
         General characteristics
        </b>
       </span>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         Crew:
        </b>
        1
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Length:
        </b>
        14.7 m (48 ft 2 in)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Wingspan" title="Wingspan">
          Wingspan
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        7.154 m (23 ft 6 in)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Height:
        </b>
        4 m (13 ft 6 in)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Wing area:
        </b>
        23 m² (247.6 ft²)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Manufacturer%27s_empty_weight" title="Manufacturer's empty weight">
          Empty weight
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        5,846 kg (12,880 lb)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Loaded weight:
        </b>
        8,725 kg (19,230 lb) with 2 × K-13A missiles
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Maximum_takeoff_weight" title="Maximum takeoff weight">
          Max. takeoff weight
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        9,800 kg (21,600 lb)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Aircraft_engine" title="Aircraft engine">
          Powerplant
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        1 ×
        <a href="/wiki/Tumansky_R-25" title="Tumansky R-25">
         Tumansky R-25
        </a>
        -300
        <a href="/wiki/Afterburner" title="Afterburner">
         afterburning
        </a>
        <a href="/wiki/Turbojet" title="Turbojet">
         turbojet
        </a>
        <ul>
         <li>
          <b>
           Dry thrust:
          </b>
          40.21 kN (9,040 lbf)
         </li>
         <li>
          <b>
           Thrust with
           <a href="/wiki/Afterburner" title="Afterburner">
            afterburner
           </a>
           :
          </b>
          69.62 kN (15,650 lbf)
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       <span style="font-size: 120%;">
        <b>
         Performance
        </b>
       </span>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/V_speeds#Regulatory_V-speeds" title="V speeds">
          Maximum speed
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        <br/>
        <ul>
         <li>
          <b>
           At sea level:
          </b>
          <a href="/wiki/Mach_number" title="Mach number">
           Mach
          </a>
          1.05 (1,300 km/h; 808 mph)
         </li>
         <li>
          <b>
           At 13,000 m (42,640 ft):
          </b>
          Mach 1.76, High altitude: Mach 1.8 (1,912 km/h, 1,032 knots) (2,175 km/h; 1,351 mph)
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Range_(aeronautics)" title="Range (aeronautics)">
          Range
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        1,470 km (910 mi; 790 nmi) at 10,000 m (32,800 ft) with 2 × K-13A missiles and 800 l (180 imp gal; 210 US gal)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Ceiling_(aeronautics)" title="Ceiling (aeronautics)">
          Service ceiling
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        17,500 m (57,400 ft)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Rate_of_climb" title="Rate of climb">
          Rate of climb
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        225 m/s (44,280 ft/min)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Wing_loading" title="Wing loading">
          Wing loading
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        452.2 kg/m² (92.7 lb/f²)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Maximum
         <i>
          g
         </i>
         -load:
        </b>
        8.5 g
        <br/>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Landing speed:
        </b>
        350 km/h (190 kn), usually with a
        <a href="/wiki/Drogue_parachute" title="Drogue parachute">
         drogue parachute
        </a>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-awClose_142-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-awClose-142">
          [139]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       <span style="font-size: 120%;">
        <b>
         Armament
        </b>
       </span>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         Guns:
        </b>
        1 × internal
        <a href="/wiki/23%C3%97115mm" title="23×115mm">
         23 mm
        </a>
        <a href="/wiki/Gryazev-Shipunov_GSh-23" title="Gryazev-Shipunov GSh-23">
         Gryazev-Shipunov GSh-23
        </a>
        L
        <a href="/wiki/Autocannon" title="Autocannon">
         autocannon
        </a>
        with 200 rounds
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Hardpoint" title="Hardpoint">
          Hardpoints
         </a>
         :
        </b>
        4 with a capacity of up to 2,000 kg (4,400 lb) of stores and provisions to carry combinations of:
        <ul>
         <li>
          <b>
           Rockets:
          </b>
          <a href="/wiki/S-24_rocket" title="S-24 rocket">
           S-24
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          <b>
           Missiles:
          </b>
          <br/>
          <ul>
           <li>
            <a href="/wiki/Air-to-air_missile" title="Air-to-air missile">
             Air-to-air missiles
            </a>
            :
            <ul>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/K-13_(missile)" title="K-13 (missile)">
               K-13
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/K-5_(missile)" title="K-5 (missile)">
               K-5
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/R-60_(missile)" title="R-60 (missile)">
               R-60
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/R-73_(missile)" title="R-73 (missile)">
               R-73
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/R-77" title="R-77">
               R-77
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/R-27_(air-to-air_missile)" title="R-27 (air-to-air missile)">
               R-27
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </li>
           <li>
            <a href="/wiki/Air-to-surface_missile" title="Air-to-surface missile">
             Air-to-surface missiles
            </a>
            :
            <ul>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/Kh-23_Grom" title="Kh-23 Grom">
               Kh-66 Grom
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/Kh-25" title="Kh-25">
               Kh-25
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="/wiki/Kh-31" title="Kh-31">
               Kh-31
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </li>
          </ul>
         </li>
         <li>
          <b>
           Bombs:
          </b>
          <br/>
          <ul>
           <li>
            <a href="/wiki/KAB-500KR" title="KAB-500KR">
             KAB-500KR
            </a>
            TV-guided bomb
           </li>
           <li>
            4 × 500 kg (1,100 lb) bombs
           </li>
          </ul>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
      </ul>
